Striker can operate on regulated AC or 12V DC electrical systems so it works on almost anything with a wheel.</li><li>An indicator dashboard accessory (022-PDA) is available if indicators are required providing space for 4 indicator lights such as neutral and high beam.</li><li>Strikers small size and ability to display and predict potential electrical problems on almost any vehicle makes it a great choice for many applications.</li><li>WARNING</li></ul>
